return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	local L1 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.L1);
	local L2 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.L2);
	local L3 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.L3);
	local L4 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.L4);
	local L5 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.L5);
	local L6 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.L6);

	local F2 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.F2);
	local F3 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.F3);

	if enabled then
			task.spawn(function()
				pcall(function()
					while true do
					F4(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F3(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F2(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));

					F7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));

					L6(0, Color3.fromRGB(110, 153, 202));
					L7(0, Color3.fromRGB(110, 153, 202));
					wait(0.03)
					F4(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F3(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F2(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F1(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					L1(0, Color3.fromRGB(110, 153, 202));
					L2(0, Color3.fromRGB(110, 153, 202));
					L3(0, Color3.fromRGB(110, 153, 202));
					L4(1, Color3.fromRGB(110, 153, 202));

					F5(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F6(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/Community_Safety/VPD_CS_Crown_Victoria/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → Community Safety → VPD CS Crown Victoria → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;


return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Rearlights;
	
	local indicatorValue = script.Parent.Parent.State.Indicators.Value
	local indicatorOn;
	
	if indicatorValue == -1 then
		indicatorOn = brakelights.Left;
	elseif indicatorValue == 1 then
		indicatorOn = brakelights.Right
	end

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0);
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then --If disabled and no headlights
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
		end;
	elseif headlightsState then --If disabled and headlights
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/Community_Safety/VPD_CS_Crown_Victoria/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → Community Safety → VPD CS Crown Victoria → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/Community_Safety/VPD_CS_Crown_Victoria/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → Community Safety → VPD CS Crown Victoria → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Rearlights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/Community_Safety/VPD_CS_Crown_Victoria/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → Community Safety → VPD CS Crown Victoria → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();
	local indicatorRear = body.Rearlights[(side == -1) and 'Left' or 'Right'];

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			indicatorRear.Material = neonMaterial;
			indicatorRear.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0)
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			indicatorRear.Material = smoothMaterial;
			indicatorRear.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
		indicatorRear.Material = indicatorRear.Parent.Centre.Material;
		indicatorRear.Color = indicatorRear.Parent.Centre.Color;
	end;
end;

	if enabled then

			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;

		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do

			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/Community_Safety/VPD_CS_Crown_Victoria/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → Community Safety → VPD CS Crown Victoria → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
			return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
				
				local Spotlight = spotlight;
				local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
				local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
				
				local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
				
				if subevent == 'Enable' then
				
					Light.Enabled = event;
					Beam.Enabled = event;
					spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
					
				elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
					if angle == 'Left' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Right' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Halt' then
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
					end;
				end;
			end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/Community_Safety/VPD_CS_Crown_Victoria/Config/TDPatterns/Left.lua ---

--[[
    Left (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → Community Safety → VPD CS Crown Victoria → Config → TDPatterns
    Parent: TDPatterns
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
local tdModule = require(script.Parent.Parent.Modules.TdPart);

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	local M2 = tdModule(ELSModel.M2);
	local M3 = tdModule(ELSModel.M3);
	local M4 = tdModule(ELSModel.M4);
	local M5 = tdModule(ELSModel.M5);
	local M6 = tdModule(ELSModel.M6);
	local M7 = tdModule(ELSModel.M7);
	
	if enabled then
		ELSModel.M2:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M3:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M4:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M5:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M6:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M7:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		while true do
			M7(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M6(1);
			M5(1);
			M4(1);
			M3(1);
			M2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			M6(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M5(1);
			M4(1);
			M3(1);
			M2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			M5(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M4(1);
			M3(1);
			M2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			M4(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M3(1);
			M2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			M3(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			M2(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			wait(0.2);
			M7(1);
			M6(1);
			M5(1);
			M4(1);
			M3(1);
			M2(1);
		end
	else
		ELSModel.M2:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M3:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M4:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M5:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M6:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M7:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		M7(1);
		M6(1);
		M5(1);
		M4(1);
		M3(1);
		M2(1);
	end
end

    Pattern1 (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → Traffic Enforcement → VPD Collision Investigation CV → Config → ELSPatterns
    Parent: ELSPatterns
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
local elsModule = require(script.Parent.Parent.Modules.ElsPart);
return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	local X1 = elsModule(ELSModel.X1);
	local X2 = elsModule(ELSModel.X2);
	
	local G1 = elsModule(ELSModel.G1);
	local G2 = elsModule(ELSModel.G2);

	local R1 = elsModule(ELSModel.R1);
	local R2 = elsModule(ELSModel.R2);
	local R3 = elsModule(ELSModel.R3);
	local R4 = elsModule(ELSModel.R4);
	local R5 = elsModule(ELSModel.R5);
	local R6 = elsModule(ELSModel.R6);
	local R7 = elsModule(ELSModel.R7);
	local R8 = elsModule(ELSModel.R8);
	if enabled then
		task.spawn(function()
			pcall(function()
				while true do
					X1(0);
					X2(0);
					wait(0.08)
				end
			end)
		end)
		task.spawn(function()
			pcall(function()
				while true do
					G1(0);
					G2(0);
					wait(0.08)
				end
			end)
		end)
		task.spawn(function()
			pcall(function()
				while true do
					R2(1);
					R3(1);
					R4(1);
					R5(1);
					R6(1);
					R7(1);
					wait(0)
				end
			end)
		end)
		task.spawn(function()
			pcall(function()
				while true do
					R1(0);
					R8(0);
					wait(0.3)
					R1(0);
					R8(0);
					wait(0.3)
				end
			end)
		end)
	else
		G1(1);
		G2(1);
		X1(1);
		X2(1);
		R1(1);
		R2(1);
		R3(1);
		R4(1);
		R5(1);
		R6(1);
		R7(1);
		R8(1);
	end
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/Traffic_Enforcement/VPD_Collision_Investigation_CV/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → Traffic Enforcement → VPD Collision Investigation CV → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;


return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Rearlights;
	
	local indicatorValue = script.Parent.Parent.State.Indicators.Value
	local indicatorOn;
	
	if indicatorValue == -1 then
		indicatorOn = brakelights.Left;
	elseif indicatorValue == 1 then
		indicatorOn = brakelights.Right
	end

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0);
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then --If disabled and no headlights
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
		end;
	elseif headlightsState then --If disabled and headlights
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/Traffic_Enforcement/VPD_Collision_Investigation_CV/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → Traffic Enforcement → VPD Collision Investigation CV → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/Traffic_Enforcement/VPD_Collision_Investigation_CV/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → Traffic Enforcement → VPD Collision Investigation CV → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Rearlights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/Traffic_Enforcement/VPD_Collision_Investigation_CV/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → Traffic Enforcement → VPD Collision Investigation CV → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();
	local indicatorRear = body.Rearlights[(side == -1) and 'Left' or 'Right'];

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			indicatorRear.Material = neonMaterial;
			indicatorRear.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0)
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			indicatorRear.Material = smoothMaterial;
			indicatorRear.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
		indicatorRear.Material = indicatorRear.Parent.Centre.Material;
		indicatorRear.Color = indicatorRear.Parent.Centre.Color;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/Traffic_Enforcement/VPD_Collision_Investigation_CV/Config/Modules/Reverselights.lua ---

--[[
    Reverselights (ModuleScript)

local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/Traffic_Enforcement/VPD_Collision_Investigation_CV/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → Traffic Enforcement → VPD Collision Investigation CV → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
			return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
				
				local Spotlight = spotlight;
				local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
				local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
				
				local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
				
				if subevent == 'Enable' then
				
					Light.Enabled = event;
					Beam.Enabled = event;
					spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
					
				elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
					if angle == 'Left' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Right' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Halt' then
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
					end;
				end;
			end;

--[[
    Left (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → Traffic Enforcement → VPD Collision Investigation CV → Config → TDPatterns
    Parent: TDPatterns
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
local tdModule = require(script.Parent.Parent.Modules.TdPart);

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	local R7 = tdModule(ELSModel.R7);
	local R6 = tdModule(ELSModel.R6);
	local R5 = tdModule(ELSModel.R5);
	local R4 = tdModule(ELSModel.R4);
	local R3 = tdModule(ELSModel.R3);
	local R2 = tdModule(ELSModel.R2);

	if enabled then
		ELSModel.R2:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R3:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R4:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R5:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R6:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R7:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		while true do
			R7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R6(1);
			R5(1);
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			R2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R6(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R5(1);
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			R2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R6(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R5(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			R2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R6(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R5(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R4(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R3(1);
			R2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R6(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R5(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R4(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R3(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R6(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R5(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R4(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R3(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R2(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			wait(0.2);
			R7(1);
			R6(1);
			R5(1);
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			R2(1);
			wait(0.3);
		end
	else
		ELSModel.R2:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R3:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R4:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R5:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R6:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.R7:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		R7(1);
		R6(1);
		R5(1);
		R4(1);
		R3(1);
		R2(1);
	end
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/Traffic_Enforcement/VPD_TE_Charger/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → Traffic Enforcement → VPD TE Charger → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/Traffic_Enforcement/VPD_TE_Charger/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → Traffic Enforcement → VPD TE Charger → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/Traffic_Enforcement/VPD_TE_Charger/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → Traffic Enforcement → VPD TE Charger → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/Traffic_Enforcement/VPD_TE_Charger/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → Traffic Enforcement → VPD TE Charger → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/Traffic_Enforcement/VPD_TE_Charger/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → Traffic Enforcement → VPD TE Charger → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
			return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
				
				local Spotlight = spotlight;
				local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
				local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
				
				local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
				
				if subevent == 'Enable' then
				
					Light.Enabled = event;
					Beam.Enabled = event;
					spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
					
				elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
					if angle == 'Left' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Right' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Halt' then
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
					end;
				end;
			end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/Traffic_Enforcement/VPD_TE_Charger/Config/TDPatterns/Left.lua ---

--[[
    Left (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → Traffic Enforcement → VPD TE Charger → Config → TDPatterns
    Parent: TDPatterns
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
local tdModule = require(script.Parent.Parent.Modules.TdPart);

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	local M2 = tdModule(ELSModel.M2);
	local M3 = tdModule(ELSModel.M3);
	local M4 = tdModule(ELSModel.M4);
	local M5 = tdModule(ELSModel.M5);
	local M6 = tdModule(ELSModel.M6);
	local M7 = tdModule(ELSModel.M7);
	
	if enabled then
		ELSModel.M2:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M3:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M4:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M5:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M6:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M7:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		while true do
			M7(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M6(1);
			M5(1);
			M4(1);
			M3(1);
			M2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			M6(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M5(1);
			M4(1);
			M3(1);
			M2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			M5(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M4(1);
			M3(1);
			M2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			M4(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M3(1);
			M2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			M3(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			M2(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			wait(0.2);
			M7(1);
			M6(1);
			M5(1);
			M4(1);
			M3(1);
			M2(1);
		end
	else
		ELSModel.M2:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M3:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M4:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M5:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M6:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M7:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		M7(1);
		M6(1);
		M5(1);
		M4(1);
		M3(1);
		M2(1);
	end
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/Traffic_Enforcement/VPD_TE_Explorer/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → Traffic Enforcement → VPD TE Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/Traffic_Enforcement/VPD_TE_Explorer/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → Traffic Enforcement → VPD TE Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/Traffic_Enforcement/VPD_TE_Explorer/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → Traffic Enforcement → VPD TE Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
			v.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
			v.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		end;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
			v.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
			v.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		end;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/Traffic_Enforcement/VPD_TE_Explorer/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → Traffic Enforcement → VPD TE Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;

	if enabled then

			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do

			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → Traffic Enforcement → VPD TE Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51
]]
return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
	
	local Spotlight = spotlight;
	local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
	local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
	
	local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
	
	if subevent == 'Enable' then
	
		Light.Enabled = event;
		Beam.Enabled = event;
		spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
		
	elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
		if angle == 'Left' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Right' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Halt' then
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/Traffic_Enforcement/VPD_TE_Explorer/Config/Modules/TdPart.lua ---

--[[
    TdPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → Traffic Enforcement → VPD TE Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		part.Transparency = (transparency)
		if colour then
			if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
				part.BrickColor = colour;
			elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
				part.Color = colour;
			end;
		end;
		if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
			local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
			a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
			if colour then
				a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
			end
		end;
	end;
end

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/Traffic_Enforcement/VPD_TE_Explorer/Config/TDPatterns/Left.lua ---

--[[
    Left (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → Traffic Enforcement → VPD TE Explorer → Config → TDPatterns
    Parent: TDPatterns
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51
]]
local tdModule = require(script.Parent.Parent.Modules.TdPart);

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	local M2 = tdModule(ELSModel.M2);
	local M3 = tdModule(ELSModel.M3);
	local M4 = tdModule(ELSModel.M4);
	local M5 = tdModule(ELSModel.M5);
	local M6 = tdModule(ELSModel.M6);
	local M7 = tdModule(ELSModel.M7);
	
	if enabled then
		ELSModel.M2:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M3:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M4:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M5:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M6:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M7:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		while true do
			M7(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M6(1);
			M5(1);
			M4(1);
			M3(1);
			M2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			M6(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M5(1);
			M4(1);
			M3(1);
			M2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			M5(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M4(1);
			M3(1);
			M2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			M4(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M3(1);
			M2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			M3(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			M2(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			wait(0.2);
			M7(1);
			M6(1);
			M5(1);
			M4(1);
			M3(1);
			M2(1);
		end
	else
		ELSModel.M2:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M3:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M4:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M5:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M6:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M7:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		M7(1);
		M6(1);
		M5(1);
		M4(1);
		M3(1);
		M2(1);
	end
end

local tdModule = require(script.Parent.Parent.Modules.TdPart);

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	local M2 = tdModule(ELSModel.M2);
	local M3 = tdModule(ELSModel.M3);
	local M4 = tdModule(ELSModel.M4);
	local M5 = tdModule(ELSModel.M5);
	local M6 = tdModule(ELSModel.M6);
	local M7 = tdModule(ELSModel.M7);

	if enabled then
		ELSModel.M2:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M3:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M4:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M5:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M6:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M7:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		while true do
			M7(1);
			M6(1);
			M5(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M4(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M3(1);
			M2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			M7(1)
			M6(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M3(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			M7(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M2(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			wait(0.3);
			M7(1);
			M6(1);
			M5(1);
			M4(1);
			M3(1);
			M2(1);
			wait(0.3);
		end
	else
		ELSModel.M2:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M3:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M4:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M5:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M6:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M7:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		M7(1);
		M6(1);
		M5(1);
		M4(1);
		M3(1);
		M2(1);
	end
end

	end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/Traffic_Enforcement/VPD_TE_F-150/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → Traffic Enforcement → VPD TE F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/Traffic_Enforcement/VPD_TE_F-150/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → Traffic Enforcement → VPD TE F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → Traffic Enforcement → VPD TE F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/Traffic_Enforcement/VPD_TE_F-150/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → Traffic Enforcement → VPD TE F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/Traffic_Enforcement/VPD_TE_F-150/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → Traffic Enforcement → VPD TE F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51
]]
return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
	
	local Spotlight = spotlight;
	local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
	local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
	
	local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
	
	if subevent == 'Enable' then
	
		Light.Enabled = event;
		Beam.Enabled = event;
		spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
		
	elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
		if angle == 'Left' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Right' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Halt' then
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/Traffic_Enforcement/VPD_TE_F-150/Config/Modules/TdPart.lua ---

--[[
    TdPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → Traffic Enforcement → VPD TE F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		part.Transparency = (transparency)
		if colour then
			if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
				part.BrickColor = colour;
			elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
				part.Color = colour;
			end;
		end;
		if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
			local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
			a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
			if colour then
				a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
			end
		end;
	end;
end

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/Traffic_Enforcement/VPD_TE_F-150/Config/TDPatterns/Left.lua ---

--[[
    Left (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → Traffic Enforcement → VPD TE F-150 → Config → TDPatterns
    Parent: TDPatterns
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51
]]
local tdModule = require(script.Parent.Parent.Modules.TdPart);

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	local M2 = tdModule(ELSModel.M2);
	local M3 = tdModule(ELSModel.M3);
	local M4 = tdModule(ELSModel.M4);
	local M5 = tdModule(ELSModel.M5);
	local M6 = tdModule(ELSModel.M6);
	local M7 = tdModule(ELSModel.M7);
	
	if enabled then
		ELSModel.M2:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M3:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M4:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M5:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M6:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M7:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		while true do
			M7(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M6(1);
			M5(1);
			M4(1);
			M3(1);
			M2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			M6(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M5(1);
			M4(1);
			M3(1);
			M2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			M5(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M4(1);
			M3(1);
			M2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			M4(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M3(1);
			M2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			M3(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			M2(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			wait(0.2);
			M7(1);
			M6(1);
			M5(1);
			M4(1);
			M3(1);
			M2(1);
		end
	else
		ELSModel.M2:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M3:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M4:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M5:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M6:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M7:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		M7(1);
		M6(1);
		M5(1);
		M4(1);
		M3(1);
		M2(1);
	end
end

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_14_Charger/VPD_14_Charger/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD 14' Charger → VPD '14 Charger → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;


return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Rearlights;

	local centre = brakelights.Centre;
	local top = brakelights.Top;

	local indicatorValue = script.Parent.Parent.State.Indicators.Value
	local indicatorOn;

	if indicatorValue == -1 then
		indicatorOn = brakelights.Left;
	elseif indicatorValue == 1 then
		indicatorOn = brakelights.Right
	end

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then --If disabled and no headlights
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
		end;
		brakelights.Top.Material = smoothMaterial;
	elseif headlightsState then --If disabled and headlights
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
		end;
		brakelights.Top.Material = smoothMaterial;
		brakelights.Top.Light.Enabled = false;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_14_Charger/VPD_14_Charger/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD 14' Charger → VPD '14 Charger → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_14_Charger/VPD_14_Charger/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD 14' Charger → VPD '14 Charger → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Rearlights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v.Name ~= 'Top' then
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v.Name ~= 'Top' then
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_14_Charger/VPD_14_Charger/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD 14' Charger → VPD '14 Charger → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
local headlightState = script.Parent.Parent.State.Headlights;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();
	local indicatorRear = body.Rearlights[(side == -1) and 'Left' or 'Right'];

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			indicatorRear.Material = neonMaterial;
			indicatorRear.Light.Enabled = true;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			indicatorRear.Material = smoothMaterial;
			indicatorRear.Light.Enabled = false;
			wait(0.5);
		end; 
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	else
		for _,v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
		indicatorRear.Material = (headlightState.Value == true and neonMaterial or smoothMaterial);
		indicatorRear.Light.Enabled = headlightState.Value;
	end;
end;

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_14_Charger/VPD_14_Charger/Config/Modules/Reverselights.lua ---

--[[
    Reverselights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD 14' Charger → VPD '14 Charger → Config → Modules

    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51

local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_14_Charger/VPD_14_Charger/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD 14' Charger → VPD '14 Charger → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51
]]
return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
	
	local Spotlight = spotlight;
	local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
	local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
	
	local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
	
	if subevent == 'Enable' then
	
		Light.Enabled = event;
		Beam.Enabled = event;
		spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
		
	elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
		if angle == 'Left' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Right' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Halt' then
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
		end;
	end;
end;

	local M4 = tdModule(ELSModel.M4);

		ELSModel.M2:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M3:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M4:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M5:SetAttribute('TD', true);

		ELSModel.M7:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		while true do
			M7(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M6(1);
			M5(1);
			M4(1);
			M3(1);
			M2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			M6(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M5(1);
			M4(1);
			M3(1);
			M2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			M5(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M4(1);
			M3(1);
			M2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			M4(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M3(1);
			M2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			M3(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			M2(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			wait(0.2);
			M7(1);
			M6(1);
			M5(1);
			M4(1);
			M3(1);
			M2(1);
		end
	else
		ELSModel.M2:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M3:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M4:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M5:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M6:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M7:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		M7(1);
		M6(1);
		M5(1);
		M4(1);
		M3(1);
		M2(1);

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_14_Charger/VPD_14_Unmarked_Charger/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD 14' Charger → VPD '14 Unmarked Charger → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;


return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Rearlights;

	local centre = brakelights.Centre;
	local top = brakelights.Top;

	local indicatorValue = script.Parent.Parent.State.Indicators.Value
	local indicatorOn;

	if indicatorValue == -1 then
		indicatorOn = brakelights.Left;
	elseif indicatorValue == 1 then
		indicatorOn = brakelights.Right
	end

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then --If disabled and no headlights
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
		end;
		brakelights.Top.Material = smoothMaterial;
	elseif headlightsState then --If disabled and headlights
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
		end;
		brakelights.Top.Material = smoothMaterial;
		brakelights.Top.Light.Enabled = false;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_14_Charger/VPD_14_Unmarked_Charger/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD 14' Charger → VPD '14 Unmarked Charger → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_14_Charger/VPD_14_Unmarked_Charger/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD 14' Charger → VPD '14 Unmarked Charger → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Rearlights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v.Name ~= 'Top' then
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v.Name ~= 'Top' then
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_14_Charger/VPD_14_Unmarked_Charger/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD 14' Charger → VPD '14 Unmarked Charger → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
local headlightState = script.Parent.Parent.State.Headlights;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();
	local indicatorRear = body.Rearlights[(side == -1) and 'Left' or 'Right'];

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			indicatorRear.Material = neonMaterial;
			indicatorRear.Light.Enabled = true;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			indicatorRear.Material = smoothMaterial;
			indicatorRear.Light.Enabled = false;
			wait(0.5);
		end; 
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	else
		for _,v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
		indicatorRear.Material = (headlightState.Value == true and neonMaterial or smoothMaterial);
		indicatorRear.Light.Enabled = headlightState.Value;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_14_Charger/VPD_14_Unmarked_Charger/Config/Modules/Reverselights.lua ---

--[[
    Reverselights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD 14' Charger → VPD '14 Unmarked Charger → Config → Modules

    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51

local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do

			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_14_Charger/VPD_14_Unmarked_Charger/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD 14' Charger → VPD '14 Unmarked Charger → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51
]]
return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
	
	local Spotlight = spotlight;
	local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
	local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
	
	local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
	
	if subevent == 'Enable' then
	
		Light.Enabled = event;
		Beam.Enabled = event;
		spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
		
	elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
		if angle == 'Left' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Right' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Halt' then
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
		end;
	end;
end;

	local M3 = tdModule(ELSModel.M3);
	local M4 = tdModule(ELSModel.M4);

		ELSModel.M3:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M4:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M5:SetAttribute('TD', true);

		ELSModel.M7:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		while true do
			M7(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M6(1);
			M5(1);
			M4(1);
			M3(1);
			M2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			M6(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M5(1);
			M4(1);
			M3(1);
			M2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			M5(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M4(1);
			M3(1);
			M2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			M4(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M3(1);
			M2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			M3(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			M2(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			wait(0.2);
			M7(1);
			M6(1);
			M5(1);
			M4(1);
			M3(1);
			M2(1);
		end
	else
		ELSModel.M2:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M3:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M4:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M5:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M6:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M7:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		M7(1);
		M6(1);
		M5(1);
		M4(1);
		M3(1);
		M2(1);

end
